		 dimensions:
			 NumberReservoirs=5;

			 TotalNumberPieces=11;

			 double DeltaRampDown(NumberIntervals,NumberArcs);
			 double MinFlow(NumberIntervals,NumberArcs);
			 double MaxFlow(NumberIntervals,NumberArcs);
			 double MinPower(NumberIntervals,NumberArcs);
			 double MaxPower(NumberIntervals,NumberArcs);

			 double LinearTerm(TotalNumberPieces);
			 double ConstantTerm(TotalNumberPieces);
		 // group attributes:
				 :type = "HydroUnitBlock" ;
		 data:
			 StartArc = 0,1,2,2,3,4 ;
			 EndArc = 1,2,3,3,4,5 ;

			 Inflows=
